  ch.swisstopo.hiks-siegfried.index
    DATA:           the_geom from (
        WITH box (geom) AS (SELECT !BOX! as geom)
        select
            gid
            , kbnum
            , location_bgdi
            , the_geom
        from box, historische_karten h
            WHERE produkt in ('ta25','ta50') and bgdi_erstausgabe is true
            and h.the_geom && box.geom
            order by produkt desc
     ) as nofx using unique gid using srid=2056
      SQL_SUBQUERY: ( WITH box (geom) AS (SELECT !BOX! as geom) select gid , kbnum , location_bgdi , the_geom from box, historische_karten h WHERE produkt in ('ta25','ta50') and bgdi_erstausgabe is true and h.the_geom && box.geom order by produkt desc )
        --ERR parsing of sql subquery failed

                    initial_power,

                    plant_type_en,
                    plant_type_fr,
                    plant_type_it,
                    array_to_string(detail_date, ', ') AS detail_date,
                    array_to_string(detail_power, ', ') AS detail_power,
                    array_to_string(detail_inclination, ', ') AS detail_inclination,
                    array_to_string(detail_plant_type_de, ', ') AS detail_plant_type_de,
                    array_to_string(detail_plant_type_en, ', ') AS detail_plant_type_en,
                    array_to_string(detail_plant_type_fr, ', ') AS detail_plant_type_fr,
                    array_to_string(detail_plant_type_it, ', ') AS detail_plant_type_it,

                    array_to_string(detail_orientation_en, ', ') AS detail_orientation_en,

sources/wms-mapfile_include/ch.swisstopo.lubis-luftbilder_schwarzweiss.map
  ch.swisstopo.lubis-luftbilder_schwarzweiss
    DATA:           geom from (
    SELECT
        the_geom as geom
        , ebkey as id
        , filename
        , inventarnummer
        , flugdatum
        , flughoehe
        , ebkey
        , filmart
        , firma
        , filesize_mb
        , bildnummer
        , bgdi_flugjahr
        , bgdi_flugjahr as year
        , orientierung
        , rotation
        , orthophoto
        , originalsize
        , ort
        , massstab
        , x
        , y

sources/wms-mapfile_include/ch.swisstopo.geologie-gisgeol-linien.map
  ch.swisstopo.geologie-gisgeol-linien
    DATA:           the_geom from (SELECT  gid, bgdi_data_status, count, pdf_url, year, doccreation_date, ST_LineSubstring(the_geom, %splitdistance%*n/length,
        CASE
          WHEN %splitdistance%*(n+1) < length THEN %splitdistance%*(n+1)/length
          ELSE 1
        END) AS the_geom
    FROM
        (SELECT gid, bgdi_data_status, count, pdf_url, year, doccreation_date, ST_LineMerge(geol.view_gisgeol_lines.the_geom) AS the_geom, ST_Length(geol.view_gisgeol_lines.the_geom) AS length
        FROM geol.view_gisgeol_lines order by pdf_url asc) AS t
    CROSS JOIN generate_series(0,250) AS n WHERE n*%splitdistance%/length < 1) as blabla USING UNIQUE gid USING srid=2056
      SCALETOKENS:  [{'__type__': 'scaletoken', 'name': '%splitdistance%', 'values': {'0': '100', '5000': '250', '10000': '750', '25000': '1000', '49000': '5000', '__type__': 'values'}}]
      SQL_SUBQUERY: (SELECT gid, bgdi_data_status, count, pdf_url, year, doccreation_date, ST_LineSubstring(the_geom, 100*n/length, CASE WHEN 100*(n+1) < length THEN 100*(n+1)/length ELSE 1 END) AS the_geom FROM (SELECT gid, bgdi_data_status, count, pdf_url, year, doccreation_date, ST_LineMerge(geol.view_gisgeol_lines.the_geom) AS the_geom, ST_Length(geol.view_gisgeol_lines.the_geom) AS length FROM geol.view_gisgeol_lines order by pdf_url asc) AS t CROSS JOIN generate_series(0,250) AS n WHERE n*100/length < 1)
        TABLE:      GENERATE_SERIES(0, 250) AS n
        TABLE:      geol.view_gisgeol_lines

sources/wms-mapfile_include/ch.bafu.bundesinventare-hochmoore.map
  ch.bafu.bundesinventare-hochmoore
    DATA:           the_geom from (
SELECT
  %geometry% as the_geom,
  bgdi_id,
  hochmoore_type,
  objnummer,
  name,
  hm_ke,
  shape_area / 10000 as shape_area,
  refobjblat,
  unit_de,
  unit_fr,
  unit_it,
  hochmoore_type_de,
  hochmoore_type_fr,
  hochmoore_type_it
from
  bundinv.hochmoore
    ) as data using unique bgdi_id using srid=2056
      SCALETOKENS:  [{'__type__': 'scaletoken', 'name': '%geometry%', 'values': {'0': 'the_geom', '300000': 'st_simplify(the_geom,20)', '1500000': 'st_simplify(the_geom,50)', '__type__': 'values'}}]
      SQL_SUBQUERY: ( SELECT the_geom as the_geom, bgdi_id, hochmoore_type, objnummer, name, hm_ke, shape_area / 10000 as shape_area, refobjblat, unit_de, unit_fr, unit_it, hochmoore_type_de, hochmoore_type_fr, hochmoore_type_it from bundinv.hochmoore )
        TABLE:      bundinv.hochmoore

    SELECT
        the_geom as geom
        , image_number
        , inventory_number
        , day
        , month
        , year
        , bgdi_date
        , substr(year::text,3,4) as bgdi_label
    from swisstopo_terrestrial.bilder
    ) AS bla USING UNIQUE inventory_number USING SRID=2056
      SQL_SUBQUERY: ( SELECT the_geom as geom , image_number , inventory_number , day , month , year , bgdi_date , substr(year::text,3,4) as bgdi_label from swisstopo_terrestrial.bilder )
        TABLE:      swisstopo_terrestrial.bilder
  ch.swisstopo.lubis-terrestrische_aufnahmen_getfeatureinfo
    DATA:           the_geom from (
        SELECT
            v.inventory_number as id
            , v.objectid as inventarnummer
            , v.image_number
            , v.bgdi_flugdatum as flugdatum
            , v.year as bgdi_flugjahr
            , v.filmart
            , v.operate_name as ort
            , v.station
            , v.base_uuid
            , v.easting as x
            , v.northing as y
            , v.format as medium_format
            , v.filesize_mb
            , v.filename
            , v.bgdi_imagemode
            , v.image_height
            , v.image_width
            , v.smapshot_id
            , v.the_geom
            , b.bgdi_date
            , b.inventory_number
        from swisstopo_terrestrial.view_bilder v left join swisstopo_terrestrial.bilder b on v.objectid = b.inventory_number

    ) AS bla USING UNIQUE inventory_number USING SRID=2056
      SQL_SUBQUERY: ( SELECT v.inventory_number as id , v.objectid as inventarnummer , v.image_number , v.bgdi_flugdatum as flugdatum , v.year as bgdi_flugjahr , v.filmart , v.operate_name as ort , v.station , v.base_uuid , v.easting as x , v.northing as y , v.format as medium_format , v.filesize_mb , v.filename , v.bgdi_imagemode , v.image_height , v.image_width , v.smapshot_id , v.the_geom , b.bgdi_date , b.inventory_number from swisstopo_terrestrial.view_bilder v left join swisstopo_terrestrial.bilder b on v.objectid = b.inventory_number )
        TABLE:      swisstopo_terrestrial.view_bilder AS v
        TABLE:      swisstopo_terrestrial.bilder AS b

            SELECT
                w.*,
                e.gesamtflaeche,
                e.min_z,
                e.max_z,
                e.mean_z,
                e.anteil_ch,
                e.as_siedlungsflaechen,
                e.as_landwirtschaftsflaechen,
                e.as_bestockteflaechen,
                e.as_unproduktiveflaechen,
                e.clc_bebauteflaechen,
                e.clc_landwirtschaft,
                e.clc_waelder,
                e.clc_feuchtflaechen,
                e.clc_wasserflaechen

            LEFT JOIN wasser.teileinzugsgebiete_2_ext e USING (ezgnr)
        ) as data using unique bgdi_id using srid=2056

        TABLE:      wasser.teileinzugsgebiete_2 AS w
        TABLE:      wasser.teileinzugsgebiete_2_ext AS e

    DATA:           the_geom FROM (SELECT bgdi_id, bgdi_id as id, inventar_nr, kanton, standort, bezeichnung, kategorie, thema, zeitraum, form, baujahr, link_zum_objekt, link_zum_gesamtinventar, kat_nr, the_geom FROM militaer.armee_kriegsdenkmaeler) as blabla using unique bgdi_id using srid=2056
      SQL_SUBQUERY: (SELECT bgdi_id, bgdi_id as id, inventar_nr, kanton, standort, bezeichnung, kategorie, thema, zeitraum, form, baujahr, link_zum_objekt, link_zum_gesamtinventar, kat_nr, the_geom FROM militaer.armee_kriegsdenkmaeler)
        TABLE:      militaer.armee_kriegsdenkmaeler

sources/wms-mapfile_include/ch.blw.bodeneignung-kulturland.map
  ch.blw.bodeneignung-kulturland
    DATA:           the_geom from (SELECT the_geom, ku_code, bgdi_id, eignungsei, farbe from blw.bodeneignung) as data using unique bgdi_id using srid=2056
      SQL_SUBQUERY: (SELECT the_geom, ku_code, bgdi_id, eignungsei, farbe from blw.bodeneignung)
        TABLE:      blw.bodeneignung

sources/wms-mapfile_include/ch.bfe.statistik-wasserkraftanlagen.map
  ch.bfe.statistik-wasserkraftanlagen
    DATA:           the_geom FROM (SELECT the_geom, wastanumber, name, location, canton, beginningofoperation, endofoperation, hydropowerplanttype, hydropowerplanttype_de, hydropowerplanttype_fr, hydropowerplanttype_it, hydropowerplantoperationalstatus_de, hydropowerplantoperationalstatus_fr, hydropowerplantoperationalstatus_it FROM bfe.statistik_wasserkraftanlagen_powerplant order by display_order) AS blabla using unique wastanumber using srid=2056
      SQL_SUBQUERY: (SELECT the_geom, wastanumber, name, location, canton, beginningofoperation, endofoperation, hydropowerplanttype, hydropowerplanttype_de, hydropowerplanttype_fr, hydropowerplanttype_it, hydropowerplantoperationalstatus_de, hydropowerplantoperationalstatus_fr, hydropowerplantoperationalstatus_it FROM bfe.statistik_wasserkraftanlagen_powerplant order by display_order)
        TABLE:      bfe.statistik_wasserkraftanlagen_powerplant

sources/wms-mapfile_include/ch.bfe.projektierungszonen-starkstromanlagen_v2_0.oereb.map
  ch.bfe.projektierungszonen-starkstromanlagen_v2_0.oereb
    DATA:           the_geom from (SELECT  bgdi_id, the_geom, stabil_id, text_aussage_%lang% as text_aussage, text_thema_%lang% as text_thema, text_rechtsstatus_%lang% as text_rechtsstatus, publiziertab, publiziertbis, text_amt_%lang% as text_amt from bfe.projektierungszonen_starkstromanlagen_v2_0_oereb WHERE rechtsstatus LIKE 'inKraft') as data using unique stabil_id using srid=2056
      SQL_SUBQUERY: (SELECT bgdi_id, the_geom, stabil_id, text_aussage_de as text_aussage, text_thema_de as text_thema, text_rechtsstatus_de as text_rechtsstatus, publiziertab, publiziertbis, text_amt_de as text_amt from bfe.projektierungszonen_starkstromanlagen_v2_0_oereb WHERE rechtsstatus LIKE 'inKraft')
        TABLE:      bfe.projektierungszonen_starkstromanlagen_v2_0_oereb
